\texttt{{-} Take sack of dried sage? Can't hold both, but can drop water after using water. So:} \\
\texttt{   1. Take vial water, go to kitchen, open cauldron, add three drops, then drop water (or keep but not needed).} \\
\texttt{   2. Return to cellar, take red berries (inventory recipe + berries), go to kitchen, add one berry, drop berries.} \\
\texttt{   3. Return, take dried sage, go, add pinch, drop.} \\
\texttt{   4. Return, take mushroom caps (tin), go, add two caps, drop.} \\
\texttt{{-} Stir, drink.} \\
\\ 
\texttt{Let's execute steps.> take vial of water  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to hallway  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to kitchen  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> open cauldron  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> add three drops of water from vial of water to cauldron  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> drop vial of water  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to hallway  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to storage room  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to cellar  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> take bowl of red berries  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to hallway  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to kitchen  } \\
\\

\\

\\ 
\texttt{> go to hallway  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to storage room  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to cellar  } \\
\\

\\ 
\texttt{> go to hallway  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to kitchen  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> add a pinch of dried sage to cauldron  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> drop sack of dried sage  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to hallway  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to storage room  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to cellar  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> take tin containing two glowing mushroom caps  } \\
\\ 
\texttt{> go to hallway  } \\

\texttt{> go to kitchen  } \\
\\

\texttt{> drop tin containing two glowing mushroom caps  } \\

\texttt{> stir cauldron clockwise three times  } \\
